SELECT a."AccessId", a."AccessName", a."CreatedBy", a."CreatedDate", a."LastModificatedDate", t."ModuleId", t."AccessId", t."CodMod", t."CodModPack", t."CreatedBy", t."CreatedDate", t."Description", t."LastModificatedDate", t."ModuleName", t."ModulePackage", t."ModuleStatus", t."ProductId", t."ProductId0", t."CodProd", t."CreatedBy0", t."CreatedDate0", t."Description0", t."FileName", t."LastModificatedDate0", t."LogoFilePath", t."ProductName", t."ProductStatus", t."ProductVersion", t."PublishDate"
FROM "Accesss" AS a
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT m."ModuleId", m."AccessId", m."CodMod", m."CodModPack", m."CreatedBy", m."CreatedDate", m."Description", m."LastModificatedDate", m."ModuleName", m."ModulePackage", m."ModuleStatus", m."ProductId", p."ProductId" AS "ProductId0", p."CodProd", p."CreatedBy" AS "CreatedBy0", p."CreatedDate" AS "CreatedDate0", p."Description" AS "Description0", p."FileName", p."LastModificatedDate" AS "LastModificatedDate0", p."LogoFilePath", p."ProductName", p."ProductStatus", p."ProductVersion", p."PublishDate"
    FROM "Modules" AS m
    LEFT JOIN "Products" AS p ON m."ProductId" = p."ProductId"
) AS t ON a."AccessId" = t."AccessId"
ORDER BY a."AccessId", t."ModuleId"

2023-07-25 20:22:41.134 +01:00 [INF] Executed DbCommand (6ms) [Parameters=[], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT a."AccessId", a."AccessName", a."LastModificatedDate", m."ModuleName", m."ModuleId", (
    SELECT p."ProductName"
    FROM "Modules" AS m0
    LEFT JOIN "Products" AS p ON m0."ProductId" = p."ProductId"
    WHERE a."AccessId" = m0."AccessId"
    LIMIT 1)
FROM "Accesss" AS a
LEFT JOIN "Modules" AS m ON a."AccessId" = m."AccessId"
ORDER BY a."AccessId"
